[30;1m30 | [0m[35m            # find the 'ts' value we're looking for. The oplog_replay option[0m
[30;1m31 | [0m[35m            # can only be used when querying the oplog. Starting in MongoDB 4.4[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35m            # this option is ignored by the server as queries against the oplog[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35m            # are optimized automatically by the MongoDB query engine.[0m
